SELECT NUM_VIEWSW FROM KECO_INTEGRATED_CLIMATE_CHANGE_PROMOTION_PORTAL_ACCESS_STS WHERE NUM_VIEWSW >= 1000 ORDER BY NUM_VIEWSW DESC

SELECT DISTINCT CONNECTION_DTV FROM KECO_INTEGRATED_CLIMATE_CHANGE_PROMOTION_PORTAL_ACCESS_STS WHERE NUM_VIEWSW >= 10 ORDER BY CONNECTION_DTV DESC

SELECT CONNECTION_DTV FROM KECO_INTEGRATED_CLIMATE_CHANGE_PROMOTION_PORTAL_ACCESS_STS WHERE MENU_NUMX LIKE '23%' ORDER BY NUM_VIEWSW DESC

SELECT NUMU, MENU_NUMX FROM KECO_INTEGRATED_CLIMATE_CHANGE_PROMOTION_PORTAL_ACCESS_STS WHERE NUM_VIEWSW >= 20 OR NUM_VIEWSW <= 10

SELECT T1.POLICE_STATION, T2.IMPORTANT_CRIME FROM CNPOLICE_POLICE_PERSONAL_PERSONNEL AS T1 JOIN STS_112_REPORT_RECEPTION_CNPOLICE_GOV_OFFICE AS T2 ON T1.POLICE_STATION = T2.POLICE_STATION WHERE T1.Y_2017 >= 500 AND T2.IMPORTANT_CRIME > (SELECT AVG(IMPORTANT_CRIME) FROM STS_112_REPORT_RECEPTION_CNPOLICE_GOV_OFFICE)
SELECT T1.POLICE_STATION FROM CNPOLICE_POLICE_PERSONAL_PERSONNEL AS T1 JOIN STS_112_REPORT_RECEPTION_CNPOLICE_GOV_OFFICE AS T2 ON T1.POLICE_STATION = T2.POLICE_STATION WHERE T1.Y_2020 > T1.Y_2021 AND T2.OTHER_CRIMES > (SELECT AVG(OTHER_CRIMES) FROM STS_112_REPORT_RECEPTION_CNPOLICE_GOV_OFFICE)
SELECT POLICE_STATION, MAINTENANCE_ORDER FROM CNPOLICE_POLICE_PERSONAL_PERSONNEL AS P JOIN STS_112_REPORT_RECEPTION_CNPOLICE_GOV_OFFICE AS R ON P.POLICE_STATION = R.POLICE_STATION WHERE P.Y_2019 > P.Y_2020 AND MAINTENANCE_ORDER >= 10000
SELECT T1.POLICE_STATION, T2.TRAFFIC FROM CNPOLICE_POLICE_PERSONAL_PERSONNEL AS T1 JOIN STS_112_REPORT_RECEPTION_CNPOLICE_GOV_OFFICE AS T2 ON T1.POLICE_STATION = T2.POLICE_STATION WHERE T1.Y_2017 >= 500 AND T2.TRAFFIC >= 10000 AND T2.TRAFFIC IS NOT NULL;
SELECT T1.POLICE_STATION, T2.OTHER_POLICE_DUTIES FROM CNPOLICE_POLICE_PERSONAL_PERSONNEL AS T1 JOIN STS_112_REPORT_RECEPTION_CNPOLICE_GOV_OFFICE AS T2 ON T1.POLICE_STATION = T2.POLICE_STATION WHERE T1.Y_2018 > 500 AND T2.OTHER_POLICE_DUTIES > (SELECT AVG(OTHER_POLICE_DUTIES) FROM STS_112_REPORT_RECEPTION_CNPOLICE_GOV_OFFICE)
SELECT T1.POLICE_STATION, T2.OTHER_ORGANS_ETC FROM CNPOLICE_POLICE_PERSONAL_PERSONNEL AS T1 JOIN STS_112_REPORT_RECEPTION_CNPOLICE_GOV_OFFICE AS T2 ON T1.POLICE_STATION = T2.POLICE_STATION WHERE T1.Y_2021 > 600 AND T2.OTHER_ORGANS_ETC >= 10000
SELECT POLICE_STATION, MAX(MAINTENANCE_ORDER) FROM CNPOLICE_POLICE_PERSONAL_PERSONNEL AS T1 JOIN STS_112_REPORT_RECEPTION_CNPOLICE_GOV_OFFICE AS T2 ON T1.POLICE_STATION = T2.POLICE_STATION WHERE T1.Y_2020 > (SELECT AVG(Y_2020) FROM CNPOLICE_POLICE_PERSONAL_PERSONNEL) AND MAINTENANCE_ORDER >= 10000 GROUP BY POLICE_STATION
SELECT T1.POLICE_STATION, T2.IMPORTANT_CRIME FROM CNPOLICE_POLICE_PERSONAL_PERSONNEL AS T1 JOIN STS_112_REPORT_RECEPTION_CNPOLICE_GOV_OFFICE AS T2 ON T1.POLICE_STATION = T2.POLICE_STATION WHERE T1.Y_2021 > (SELECT AVG(Y_2017) FROM CNPOLICE_POLICE_PERSONAL_PERSONNEL) ORDER BY T2.IMPORTANT_CRIME DESC LIMIT 1
SELECT POLICE_STATION, MAINTENANCE_ORDER FROM STS_112_REPORT_RECEPTION_CNPOLICE_GOV_OFFICE WHERE POLICE_STATION IN ( SELECT POLICE_STATION FROM CNPOLICE_POLICE_PERSONAL_PERSONNEL WHERE Y_2020 > ( SELECT AVG(Y_2020) FROM CNPOLICE_POLICE_PERSONAL_PERSONNEL ) ) AND MAINTENANCE_ORDER > ( SELECT AVG(MAINTENANCE_ORDER) FROM STS_112_REPORT_RECEPTION_CNPOLICE_GOV_OFFICE )
SELECT T2.POLICE_STATION FROM CNPOLICE_POLICE_PERSONAL_PERSONNEL AS T1 JOIN STS_112_REPORT_RECEPTION_CNPOLICE_GOV_OFFICE AS T2 ON T1.POLICE_STATION = T2.POLICE_STATION WHERE T2.MAINTENANCE_ORDER > (SELECT AVG(MAINTENANCE_ORDER) FROM STS_112_REPORT_RECEPTION_CNPOLICE_GOV_OFFICE) AND T1.Y_2019 >= 700
SELECT T1.POLICE_STATION, T2.MAINTENANCE_ORDER FROM CNPOLICE_POLICE_PERSONAL_PERSONNEL AS T1 JOIN STS_112_REPORT_RECEPTION_CNPOLICE_GOV_OFFICE AS T2 ON T1.POLICE_STATION = T2.POLICE_STATION WHERE T2.IMPORTANT_CRIME < T2.OTHER_CRIMES OR T1.Y_2021 < T1.Y_2020
SELECT T1.POLICE_STATION FROM CNPOLICE_POLICE_PERSONAL_PERSONNEL AS T1 JOIN STS_112_REPORT_RECEPTION_CNPOLICE_GOV_OFFICE AS T2 ON T1.POLICE_STATION = T2.POLICE_STATION WHERE T1.Y_2019 > T2.IMPORTANT_CRIME AND T2.OTHER_CRIMES >= 10000;
SELECT AVG(Y_2017) FROM CNPOLICE_POLICE_PERSONAL_PERSONNEL AS T1 JOIN STS_112_REPORT_RECEPTION_CNPOLICE_GOV_OFFICE AS T2 ON T1.POLICE_STATION = T2.POLICE_STATION WHERE IMPORTANT_CRIME >= 3000
SELECT POLICE_STATION FROM CNPOLICE_POLICE_PERSONAL_PERSONNEL WHERE Y_2017 = (SELECT MIN(Y_2017) FROM CNPOLICE_POLICE_PERSONAL_PERSONNEL)
SELECT Y_2018, OTHER_CRIMES FROM CNPOLICE_POLICE_PERSONAL_PERSONNEL JOIN STS_112_REPORT_RECEPTION_CNPOLICE_GOV_OFFICE ON CNPOLICE_POLICE_PERSONAL_PERSONNEL.POLICE_STATION = STS_112_REPORT_RECEPTION_CNPOLICE_GOV_OFFICE.POLICE_STATION WHERE CNPOLICE_POLICE_PERSONAL_PERSONNEL.POLICE_STATION = '논산서'
SELECT T1.POLICE_STATION, T2.IMPORTANT_CRIME FROM CNPOLICE_POLICE_PERSONAL_PERSONNEL AS T1 JOIN STS_112_REPORT_RECEPTION_CNPOLICE_GOV_OFFICE AS T2 ON T1.POLICE_STATION = T2.POLICE_STATION WHERE T1.Y_2019 > T1.Y_2020 AND T2.TRAFFIC >= 5000
SELECT T2.POLICE_STATION, T2.IMPORTANT_CRIME FROM CNPOLICE_POLICE_PERSONAL_PERSONNEL AS T1 JOIN STS_112_REPORT_RECEPTION_CNPOLICE_GOV_OFFICE AS T2 ON T1.POLICE_STATION = T2.POLICE_STATION WHERE T1.Y_2017 > (SELECT AVG(Y_2017) FROM CNPOLICE_POLICE_PERSONAL_PERSONNEL) AND T2.IMPORTANT_CRIME > T2.OTHER_CRIMES
SELECT T1.POLICE_STATION, T2.MAINTENANCE_ORDER FROM CNPOLICE_POLICE_PERSONAL_PERSONNEL AS T1 JOIN STS_112_REPORT_RECEPTION_CNPOLICE_GOV_OFFICE AS T2 ON T1.POLICE_STATION = T2.POLICE_STATION WHERE T2.OTHER_CRIMES > (SELECT AVG(IMPORTANT_CRIME) FROM STS_112_REPORT_RECEPTION_CNPOLICE_GOV_OFFICE) AND T1.Y_2021 > (SELECT AVG(Y_2020) FROM CNPOLICE_POLICE_PERSONAL_PERSONNEL)
SELECT T1.POLICE_STATION, T2.OTHER_CRIMES FROM CNPOLICE_POLICE_PERSONAL_PERSONNEL AS T1 JOIN STS_112_REPORT_RECEPTION_CNPOLICE_GOV_OFFICE AS T2 ON T1.POLICE_STATION = T2.POLICE_STATION WHERE T1.Y_2018 > (SELECT AVG(Y_2018) FROM CNPOLICE_POLICE_PERSONAL_PERSONNEL) AND T2.OTHER_CRIMES > T2.MAINTENANCE_ORDER
SELECT T1.POLICE_STATION, T2.MAINTENANCE_ORDER FROM CNPOLICE_POLICE_PERSONAL_PERSONNEL AS T1 JOIN STS_112_REPORT_RECEPTION_CNPOLICE_GOV_OFFICE AS T2 ON T1.POLICE_STATION = T2.POLICE_STATION WHERE T1.Y_2019 > (SELECT AVG(Y_2019) FROM CNPOLICE_POLICE_PERSONAL_PERSONNEL) AND T2.IMPORTANT_CRIME > T2.TRAFFIC
SELECT T1.POLICE_STATION, T2.TRAFFIC FROM CNPOLICE_POLICE_PERSONAL_PERSONNEL AS T1 JOIN STS_112_REPORT_RECEPTION_CNPOLICE_GOV_OFFICE AS T2 ON T1.POLICE_STATION = T2.POLICE_STATION WHERE T1.Y_2019 > (SELECT AVG(Y_2019) FROM CNPOLICE_POLICE_PERSONAL_PERSONNEL) AND T2.TRAFFIC > (SELECT AVG(TRAFFIC) FROM STS_112_REPORT_RECEPTION_CNPOLICE_GOV_OFFICE)
SELECT T1.POLICE_STATION FROM CNPOLICE_POLICE_PERSONAL_PERSONNEL AS T1 JOIN STS_112_REPORT_RECEPTION_CNPOLICE_GOV_OFFICE AS T2 ON T1.POLICE_STATION = T2.POLICE_STATION WHERE T1.Y_2019 >= 819 OR T2.IMPORTANT_CRIME > (SELECT AVG(OTHER_CRIMES) FROM STS_112_REPORT_RECEPTION_CNPOLICE_GOV_OFFICE)
SELECT POLICE_STATION, (Y_2017 / OTHER_CRIMES) AS POPULATION_PER_OFFICER_2017, (Y_2019 / OTHER_CRIMES) AS POPULATION_PER_OFFICER_2019 FROM CNPOLICE_POLICE_PERSONAL_PERSONNEL JOIN STS_112_REPORT_RECEPTION_CNPOLICE_GOV_OFFICE ON CNPOLICE_POLICE_PERSONAL_PERSONNEL.POLICE_STATION = STS_112_REPORT_RECEPTION_CNPOLICE_GOV_OFFICE.POLICE_STATION WHERE OTHER_CRIMES >= 10000
SELECT T1.POLICE_STATION FROM CNPOLICE_POLICE_PERSONAL_PERSONNEL AS T1 JOIN STS_112_REPORT_RECEPTION_CNPOLICE_GOV_OFFICE AS T2 ON T1.POLICE_STATION = T2.POLICE_STATION WHERE T1.Y_2021 >= 700 OR T2.TRAFFIC > T2.MAINTENANCE_ORDER
SELECT T1.POLICE_STATION FROM CNPOLICE_POLICE_PERSONAL_PERSONNEL AS T1 JOIN STS_112_REPORT_RECEPTION_CNPOLICE_GOV_OFFICE AS T2 ON T1.POLICE_STATION = T2.POLICE_STATION WHERE T1.Y_2021 <= (SELECT AVG(Y_2021) FROM CNPOLICE_POLICE_PERSONAL_PERSONNEL) OR T2.TRAFFIC > (SELECT AVG(TRAFFIC) FROM STS_112_REPORT_RECEPTION_CNPOLICE_GOV_OFFICE)
SELECT T1.POLICE_STATION FROM CNPOLICE_POLICE_PERSONAL_PERSONNEL AS T1 JOIN STS_112_REPORT_RECEPTION_CNPOLICE_GOV_OFFICE AS T2 ON T1.POLICE_STATION = T2.POLICE_STATION WHERE T1.Y_2019 = (SELECT MAX(Y_2019) FROM CNPOLICE_POLICE_PERSONAL_PERSONNEL) OR T2.IMPORTANT_CRIME > (SELECT AVG(OTHER_CRIMES) FROM STS_112_REPORT_RECEPTION_CNPOLICE_GOV_OFFICE)
SELECT T1.POLICE_STATION FROM CNPOLICE_POLICE_PERSONAL_PERSONNEL AS T1 JOIN STS_112_REPORT_RECEPTION_CNPOLICE_GOV_OFFICE AS T2 ON T1.POLICE_STATION = T2.POLICE_STATION WHERE T1.Y_2021 / T1.Y_2017 >= 700 OR T2.OTHER_CRIMES >= 13000
SELECT T1.POLICE_STATION FROM CNPOLICE_POLICE_PERSONAL_PERSONNEL AS T1 JOIN STS_112_REPORT_RECEPTION_CNPOLICE_GOV_OFFICE AS T2 ON T1.POLICE_STATION = T2.POLICE_STATION WHERE (T1.Y_2020 = (SELECT MAX(Y_2020) FROM CNPOLICE_POLICE_PERSONAL_PERSONNEL) OR T1.Y_2021 = (SELECT MAX(Y_2021) FROM CNPOLICE_POLICE_PERSONAL_PERSONNEL)) AND T2.OTHER_CRIMES > T2.MAINTENANCE_ORDER
SELECT DISTINCT POLICE_STATION FROM CNPOLICE_POLICE_PERSONAL_PERSONNEL AS P JOIN STS_112_REPORT_RECEPTION_CNPOLICE_GOV_OFFICE AS R ON P.POLICE_STATION = R.POLICE_STATION WHERE R.OTHER_CRIMES <= (SELECT AVG(IMPORTANT_CRIME) FROM STS_112_REPORT_RECEPTION_CNPOLICE_GOV_OFFICE)
SELECT T1.POLICE_STATION FROM CNPOLICE_POLICE_PERSONAL_PERSONNEL AS T1 JOIN STS_112_REPORT_RECEPTION_CNPOLICE_GOV_OFFICE AS T2 ON T1.POLICE_STATION = T2.POLICE_STATION WHERE T1.Y_2020 > (SELECT AVG(Y_2021) FROM CNPOLICE_POLICE_PERSONAL_PERSONNEL) ORDER BY T1.POLICE_STATION DESC
SELECT T1.POLICE_STATION FROM CNPOLICE_POLICE_PERSONAL_PERSONNEL AS T1 JOIN STS_112_REPORT_RECEPTION_CNPOLICE_GOV_OFFICE AS T2 ON T1.POLICE_STATION = T2.POLICE_STATION WHERE T2.TRAFFIC >= 10000 OR T1.Y_2020 = 421 ORDER BY T1.POLICE_STATION ASC;
SELECT T1.POLICE_STATION FROM CNPOLICE_POLICE_PERSONAL_PERSONNEL AS T1 JOIN STS_112_REPORT_RECEPTION_CNPOLICE_GOV_OFFICE AS T2 ON T1.POLICE_STATION = T2.POLICE_STATION WHERE T1.Y_2017 <= 500 AND (T2.IMPORTANT_CRIME = 958 OR T2.IMPORTANT_CRIME = 1427 OR T2.IMPORTANT_CRIME = 428) AND T1.POLICE_STATION LIKE '%충청남도 경찰청%'
SELECT POLICE_STATION FROM CNPOLICE_POLICE_PERSONAL_PERSONNEL INNER JOIN STS_112_REPORT_RECEPTION_CNPOLICE_GOV_OFFICE ON CNPOLICE_POLICE_PERSONAL_PERSONNEL.POLICE_STATION = STS_112_REPORT_RECEPTION_CNPOLICE_GOV_OFFICE.POLICE_STATION WHERE TRAFFIC > MAINTENANCE_ORDER ORDER BY Y_2017 DESC;
SELECT T1.POLICE_STATION FROM CNPOLICE_POLICE_PERSONAL_PERSONNEL AS T1 JOIN STS_112_REPORT_RECEPTION_CNPOLICE_GOV_OFFICE AS T2 ON T1.POLICE_STATION = T2.POLICE_STATION WHERE T2.OTHER_POLICE_DUTIES <= 1000 ORDER BY T1.Y_2021 ASC LIMIT 1
SELECT DISTINCT POLICE_STATION FROM STS_112_REPORT_RECEPTION_CNPOLICE_GOV_OFFICE WHERE OTHER_CRIMES >= 10000 OR Y_2017 / Y_2018 >= 800

SELECT T2.POLICE_STATION FROM STS_112_REPORT_RECEPTION_CNPOLICE_GOV_OFFICE AS T1 JOIN CNPOLICE_POLICE_PERSONAL_PERSONNEL AS T2 ON T1.POLICE_STATION = T2.POLICE_STATION WHERE T1.MAINTENANCE_ORDER > 10000 OR (T1.TRAFFIC > 8000 AND T2.Y_2021 >= 700)
SELECT POLICE_STATION FROM STS_112_REPORT_RECEPTION_CNPOLICE_GOV_OFFICE WHERE IMPORTANT_CRIME >= 3000
SELECT T1.POLICE_STATION FROM CNPOLICE_POLICE_PERSONAL_PERSONNEL AS T1 JOIN STS_112_REPORT_RECEPTION_CNPOLICE_GOV_OFFICE AS T2 ON T1.POLICE_STATION = T2.POLICE_STATION WHERE T2.MAINTENANCE_ORDER <= 2000 OR T1.Y_2021 >= 700 ORDER BY T1.POLICE_STATION ASC;
SELECT T1.POLICE_STATION FROM CNPOLICE_POLICE_PERSONAL_PERSONNEL AS T1 JOIN STS_112_REPORT_RECEPTION_CNPOLICE_GOV_OFFICE AS T2 ON T1.POLICE_STATION = T2.POLICE_STATION WHERE T1.Y_2021 >= 722 OR T2.OTHER_ORGANS_ETC <= (SELECT AVG(OTHER_ORGANS_ETC) FROM STS_112_REPORT_RECEPTION_CNPOLICE_GOV_OFFICE) ORDER BY T2.TRAFFIC DESC;

SELECT DISTINCT T1.POLICE_STATION FROM CNPOLICE_POLICE_PERSONAL_PERSONNEL AS T1 JOIN STS_112_REPORT_RECEPTION_CNPOLICE_GOV_OFFICE AS T2 ON T1.POLICE_STATION = T2.POLICE_STATION WHERE T1.Y_2017 >= 808 OR T2.MAINTENANCE_ORDER <= (SELECT AVG(MAINTENANCE_ORDER) FROM STS_112_REPORT_RECEPTION_CNPOLICE_GOV_OFFICE) ORDER BY T1.POLICE_STATION DESC
SELECT T1.POLICE_STATION FROM CNPOLICE_POLICE_PERSONAL_PERSONNEL AS T1 JOIN STS_112_REPORT_RECEPTION_CNPOLICE_GOV_OFFICE AS T2 ON T1.POLICE_STATION = T2.POLICE_STATION WHERE T1.Y_2018 >= 677 OR T2.OTHER_CRIMES <= (SELECT AVG(OTHER_CRIMES) FROM STS_112_REPORT_RECEPTION_CNPOLICE_GOV_OFFICE)
SELECT T2.POLICE_STATION FROM CNPOLICE_POLICE_PERSONAL_PERSONNEL AS T1 JOIN STS_112_REPORT_RECEPTION_CNPOLICE_GOV_OFFICE AS T2 ON T1.POLICE_STATION = T2.POLICE_STATION WHERE T1.Y_2020 <= 500
SELECT POLICE_STATION FROM STS_112_REPORT_RECEPTION_CNPOLICE_GOV_OFFICE WHERE TRAFFIC = 5163 OR TRAFFIC = 7218 ORDER BY POLICE_STATION ASC

SELECT POLICE_STATION FROM STS_112_REPORT_RECEPTION_CNPOLICE_GOV_OFFICE WHERE TRAFFIC <= 5000 ORDER BY POLICE_STATION
SELECT POLICE_STATION FROM STS_112_REPORT_RECEPTION_CNPOLICE_GOV_OFFICE WHERE OTHER_CRIMES >= 7000 AND POLICE_STATION LIKE '%천안%'
SELECT POLICE_STATION FROM STS_112_REPORT_RECEPTION_CNPOLICE_GOV_OFFICE WHERE TRAFFIC < (SELECT AVG(TRAFFIC) FROM STS_112_REPORT_RECEPTION_CNPOLICE_GOV_OFFICE)
SELECT POLICE_STATION FROM STS_112_REPORT_RECEPTION_CNPOLICE_GOV_OFFICE WHERE TRAFFIC >= 10000
SELECT T1.POLICE_STATION FROM CNPOLICE_POLICE_PERSONAL_PERSONNEL AS T1 JOIN STS_112_REPORT_RECEPTION_CNPOLICE_GOV_OFFICE AS T2 ON T1.POLICE_STATION = T2.POLICE_STATION WHERE T1.Y_2020 >= 111 OR T2.OTHER_CRIMES <= (SELECT AVG(OTHER_CRIMES) FROM STS_112_REPORT_RECEPTION_CNPOLICE_GOV_OFFICE) ORDER BY T1.Y_2021 DESC
SELECT POLICE_STATION FROM CNPOLICE_POLICE_PERSONAL_PERSONNEL WHERE Y_2019 > (SELECT MAX(Y_2021) FROM CNPOLICE_POLICE_PERSONAL_PERSONNEL)
SELECT DISTINCT POLICE_STATION FROM CNPOLICE_POLICE_PERSONAL_PERSONNEL AS T1 JOIN STS_112_REPORT_RECEPTION_CNPOLICE_GOV_OFFICE AS T2 ON T1.POLICE_STATION = T2.POLICE_STATION WHERE T1.Y_2021 IN (590, 710)
SELECT T2.POLICE_STATION FROM CNPOLICE_POLICE_PERSONAL_PERSONNEL AS T1 JOIN STS_112_REPORT_RECEPTION_CNPOLICE_GOV_OFFICE AS T2 ON T1.POLICE_STATION = T2.POLICE_STATION WHERE T2.MAINTENANCE_ORDER > 24000 OR T1.Y_2019 <= 240
SELECT DISTINCT CP.POLICE_STATION, SR.IMPORTANT_CRIME FROM CNPOLICE_POLICE_PERSONAL_PERSONNEL AS CP JOIN STS_112_REPORT_RECEPTION_CNPOLICE_GOV_OFFICE AS SR ON CP.POLICE_STATION = SR.POLICE_STATION WHERE SR.IMPORTANT_CRIME <= 3300;
SELECT POLICE_STATION FROM STS_112_REPORT_RECEPTION_CNPOLICE_GOV_OFFICE WHERE IMPORTANT_CRIME = 10410 ORDER BY MAINTENANCE_ORDER ASC LIMIT 1
SELECT POLICE_STATION FROM STS_112_REPORT_RECEPTION_CNPOLICE_GOV_OFFICE ORDER BY IMPORTANT_CRIME ASC LIMIT 1
SELECT POLICE_STATION FROM STS_112_REPORT_RECEPTION_CNPOLICE_GOV_OFFICE WHERE OTHER_CRIMES > (SELECT AVG(MAINTENANCE_ORDER) FROM STS_112_REPORT_RECEPTION_CNPOLICE_GOV_OFFICE)
SELECT T2.POLICE_STATION FROM CNPOLICE_POLICE_PERSONAL_PERSONNEL AS T1 JOIN STS_112_REPORT_RECEPTION_CNPOLICE_GOV_OFFICE AS T2 ON T1.POLICE_STATION = T2.POLICE_STATION WHERE T1.Y_2021 <= 500 OR T2.TRAFFIC >= 10000 ORDER BY T2.POLICE_STATION DESC
SELECT T1.POLICE_STATION FROM CNPOLICE_POLICE_PERSONAL_PERSONNEL AS T1 JOIN STS_112_REPORT_RECEPTION_CNPOLICE_GOV_OFFICE AS T2 ON T1.POLICE_STATION = T2.POLICE_STATION WHERE T2.OTHER_ORGANS_ETC > T2.OTHER_POLICE_DUTIES AND T1.Y_2017 >= 820 GROUP BY T1.POLICE_STATION
SELECT T1.POLICE_STATION AS MIN_Y_2017, T2.POLICE_STATION AS MIN_Y_2018 FROM CNPOLICE_POLICE_PERSONAL_PERSONNEL AS T1 JOIN CNPOLICE_POLICE_PERSONAL_PERSONNEL AS T2 ON T1.Y_2017 = (SELECT MIN(Y_2017) FROM CNPOLICE_POLICE_PERSONAL_PERSONNEL) AND T2.Y_2018 = (SELECT MIN(Y_2018) FROM CNPOLICE_POLICE_PERSONAL_PERSONNEL)
SELECT POLICE_STATION FROM STS_112_REPORT_RECEPTION_CNPOLICE_GOV_OFFICE WHERE MAINTENANCE_ORDER < (SELECT MAX(IMPORTANT_CRIME) FROM STS_112_REPORT_RECEPTION_CNPOLICE_GOV_OFFICE)
SELECT T2.POLICE_STATION FROM STS_112_REPORT_RECEPTION_CNPOLICE_GOV_OFFICE AS T1 JOIN CNPOLICE_POLICE_PERSONAL_PERSONNEL AS T2 ON T1.POLICE_STATION = T2.POLICE_STATION WHERE (T1.IMPORTANT_CRIME + T1.OTHER_CRIMES) > ((SELECT AVG(IMPORTANT_CRIME + OTHER_CRIMES) FROM STS_112_REPORT_RECEPTION_CNPOLICE_GOV_OFFICE) * 2) AND T2.Y_2018 < 600
SELECT DISTINCT Y_2017 / Y_2018 FROM CNPOLICE_POLICE_PERSONAL_PERSONNEL WHERE POLICE_STATION IN (SELECT POLICE_STATION FROM STS_112_REPORT_RECEPTION_CNPOLICE_GOV_OFFICE WHERE OTHER_CRIMES >= 10000)
SELECT DISTINCT POLICE_STATION FROM STS_112_REPORT_RECEPTION_CNPOLICE_GOV_OFFICE WHERE IMPORTANT_CRIME >= 3000 AND OTHER_CRIMES >= 8000
SELECT DISTINCT T1.POLICE_STATION FROM CNPOLICE_POLICE_PERSONAL_PERSONNEL AS T1 JOIN STS_112_REPORT_RECEPTION_CNPOLICE_GOV_OFFICE AS T2 ON T1.POLICE_STATION = T2.POLICE_STATION WHERE T2.TRAFFIC >= 7200 AND T1.Y_2021 > 700
SELECT T1.Y_2017, T1.Y_2018 FROM CNPOLICE_POLICE_PERSONAL_PERSONNEL AS T1 WHERE T1.POLICE_STATION = '천안서북서'
SELECT T1.POLICE_STATION FROM CNPOLICE_POLICE_PERSONAL_PERSONNEL AS T1 JOIN STS_112_REPORT_RECEPTION_CNPOLICE_GOV_OFFICE AS T2 ON T1.POLICE_STATION = T2.POLICE_STATION WHERE (T1.Y_2017 < 600 OR T1.Y_2018 < 600) AND T2.IMPORTANT_CRIME > (SELECT AVG(IMPORTANT_CRIME) FROM STS_112_REPORT_RECEPTION_CNPOLICE_GOV_OFFICE)
SELECT POLICE_STATION FROM STS_112_REPORT_RECEPTION_CNPOLICE_GOV_OFFICE JOIN CNPOLICE_POLICE_PERSONAL_PERSONNEL ON STS_112_REPORT_RECEPTION_CNPOLICE_GOV_OFFICE.POLICE_STATION = CNPOLICE_POLICE_PERSONAL_PERSONNEL.POLICE_STATION WHERE MAINTENANCE_ORDER = (SELECT MAX(MAINTENANCE_ORDER) FROM STS_112_REPORT_RECEPTION_CNPOLICE_GOV_OFFICE) AND Y_2019 < (SELECT AVG(Y_2019) FROM CNPOLICE_POLICE_PERSONAL_PERSONNEL)
SELECT DISTINCT Y_2019 / Y_2019 FROM CNPOLICE_POLICE_PERSONAL_PERSONNEL WHERE POLICE_STATION = '서산서'
SELECT T1.POLICE_STATION FROM CNPOLICE_POLICE_PERSONAL_PERSONNEL AS T1 JOIN STS_112_REPORT_RECEPTION_CNPOLICE_GOV_OFFICE AS T2 ON T1.POLICE_STATION = T2.POLICE_STATION WHERE T1.Y_2017 < (SELECT AVG(Y_2017) FROM CNPOLICE_POLICE_PERSONAL_PERSONNEL) OR T2.OTHER_CRIMES < 8888 ORDER BY T2.IMPORTANT_CRIME DESC
SELECT POLICE_STATION FROM STS_112_REPORT_RECEPTION_CNPOLICE_GOV_OFFICE WHERE OTHER_POLICE_DUTIES <= (SELECT AVG(OTHER_POLICE_DUTIES) FROM STS_112_REPORT_RECEPTION_CNPOLICE_GOV_OFFICE)
SELECT POLICE_STATION FROM STS_112_REPORT_RECEPTION_CNPOLICE_GOV_OFFICE WHERE (IMPORTANT_CRIME < 1000 OR TRAFFIC >= 15000) AND POLICE_STATION IN (SELECT POLICE_STATION FROM CNPOLICE_POLICE_PERSONAL_PERSONNEL WHERE Y_2020 <= (SELECT AVG(Y_2020) FROM CNPOLICE_POLICE_PERSONAL_PERSONNEL))
SELECT DISTINCT T1.POLICE_STATION FROM CNPOLICE_POLICE_PERSONAL_PERSONNEL AS T1 JOIN STS_112_REPORT_RECEPTION_CNPOLICE_GOV_OFFICE AS T2 ON T1.POLICE_STATION = T2.POLICE_STATION WHERE T2.OTHER_POLICE_DUTIES < 10000 OR T1.Y_2018 < (SELECT AVG(Y_2018) FROM CNPOLICE_POLICE_PERSONAL_PERSONNEL)
SELECT DISTINCT POLICE_STATION, Y_2020/(Y_2017+Y_2018+Y_2019+Y_2020+Y_2021) AS POLICE_POPULATION_RATIO FROM CNPOLICE_POLICE_PERSONAL_PERSONNEL JOIN STS_112_REPORT_RECEPTION_CNPOLICE_GOV_OFFICE ON CNPOLICE_POLICE_PERSONAL_PERSONNEL.POLICE_STATION = STS_112_REPORT_RECEPTION_CNPOLICE_GOV_OFFICE.POLICE_STATION WHERE IMPORTANT_CRIME <= 1000 OR MAINTENANCE_ORDER >= 20000
SELECT DISTINCT POLICE_STATION FROM STS_112_REPORT_RECEPTION_CNPOLICE_GOV_OFFICE WHERE MAINTENANCE_ORDER >= 20000
SELECT DISTINCT T1.POLICE_STATION FROM CNPOLICE_POLICE_PERSONAL_PERSONNEL AS T1 JOIN STS_112_REPORT_RECEPTION_CNPOLICE_GOV_OFFICE AS T2 ON T1.POLICE_STATION = T2.POLICE_STATION WHERE T1.Y_2019 < (SELECT AVG(Y_2019) FROM CNPOLICE_POLICE_PERSONAL_PERSONNEL) OR T2.TRAFFIC < (SELECT AVG(TRAFFIC) FROM STS_112_REPORT_RECEPTION_CNPOLICE_GOV_OFFICE)
SELECT DISTINCT Y_2018 FROM CNPOLICE_POLICE_PERSONAL_PERSONNEL WHERE POLICE_STATION = '보령서'
SELECT T1.POLICE_STATION FROM CNPOLICE_POLICE_PERSONAL_PERSONNEL AS T1 JOIN STS_112_REPORT_RECEPTION_CNPOLICE_GOV_OFFICE AS T2 ON T1.POLICE_STATION = T2.POLICE_STATION WHERE T1.Y_2020 > (SELECT AVG(Y_2020) FROM CNPOLICE_POLICE_PERSONAL_PERSONNEL) AND T2.MAINTENANCE_ORDER >= 20000
SELECT T1.POLICE_STATION, T2.IMPORTANT_CRIME FROM CNPOLICE_POLICE_PERSONAL_PERSONNEL AS T1 JOIN STS_112_REPORT_RECEPTION_CNPOLICE_GOV_OFFICE AS T2 ON T1.POLICE_STATION = T2.POLICE_STATION WHERE T1.Y_2021 > T1.Y_2020 AND T2.IMPORTANT_CRIME > T2.OTHER_CRIMES
SELECT T1.POLICE_STATION FROM CNPOLICE_POLICE_PERSONAL_PERSONNEL AS T1 JOIN STS_112_REPORT_RECEPTION_CNPOLICE_GOV_OFFICE AS T2 ON T1.POLICE_STATION = T2.POLICE_STATION WHERE T1.Y_2019 > (SELECT AVG(Y_2019) FROM CNPOLICE_POLICE_PERSONAL_PERSONNEL) AND T2.IMPORTANT_CRIME >= 1500
SELECT SORTATION FROM NUM_WORKERS_KOSHA_I_MIDDLE_CLASSIFICATION WHERE Y_2004 >= 100000 AND SORTATION LIKE '%업'
SELECT Y_2005 FROM NUM_ACCIDENT_DEATHS_KOSHA_I_MIDDLE_CLASSIFICATION WHERE Y_2006 < 100000 AND LARGE_INDUSTRY = '제조업'
SELECT LARGE_INDUSTRY FROM NUM_WORKERS_KOSHA_I_MIDDLE_CLASSIFICATION WHERE Y_2008 < (SELECT AVG(Y_2008) FROM NUM_WORKERS_KOSHA_I_MIDDLE_CLASSIFICATION)
SELECT LARGE_INDUSTRY, COUNT(*) FROM NUM_WORKERS_KOSHA_I_MIDDLE_CLASSIFICATION WHERE Y_2007 < (SELECT AVG(Y_2007) FROM NUM_WORKERS_KOSHA_I_MIDDLE_CLASSIFICATION) GROUP BY LARGE_INDUSTRY 
SELECT COUNT(LARGE_INDUSTRY) FROM NUM_WORKERS_KOSHA_I_MIDDLE_CLASSIFICATION WHERE Y_2007 = (SELECT MAX(Y_2007) FROM NUM_WORKERS_KOSHA_I_MIDDLE_CLASSIFICATION) AND Y_2008 < Y_2007
SELECT DISTINCT SORTATION FROM NUM_ACCIDENT_DEATHS_KOSHA_I_MIDDLE_CLASSIFICATION WHERE Y_2010 < (SELECT AVG(Y_2010) FROM NUM_ACCIDENT_DEATHS_KOSHA_I_MIDDLE_CLASSIFICATION) ORDER BY SORTATION ASC
SELECT LARGE_INDUSTRY, AVG(Y_2012) as AVG_DEATHS_2012 FROM NUM_ACCIDENT_DEATHS_KOSHA_I_MIDDLE_CLASSIFICATION WHERE Y_2012 <= (SELECT MAX(Y_2013) FROM NUM_ACCIDENT_DEATHS_KOSHA_I_MIDDLE_CLASSIFICATION) GROUP BY LARGE_INDUSTRY HAVING AVG_DEATHS_2012 <= 0;
SELECT LARGE_INDUSTRY, Y_2014 FROM NUM_ACCIDENT_DEATHS_KOSHA_I_MIDDLE_CLASSIFICATION WHERE SORTATION IN (SELECT SORTATION FROM NUM_WORKERS_KOSHA_I_MIDDLE_CLASSIFICATION) AND Y_2014 > 10
SELECT LARGE_INDUSTRY, Y_2015 + Y_2016 AS TOTAL_DEATHS FROM NUM_ACCIDENT_DEATHS_KOSHA_I_MIDDLE_CLASSIFICATION WHERE Y_2015 + Y_2016 > 30 ORDER BY Y_2015 DESC;
SELECT T1.Y_2004, T1.Y_2005 FROM NUM_WORKERS_KOSHA_I_MIDDLE_CLASSIFICATION AS T1 JOIN NUM_ACCIDENT_DEATHS_KOSHA_I_MIDDLE_CLASSIFICATION AS T2 ON T1.SORTATION = T2.SORTATION WHERE T2.Y_2007 = (SELECT MAX(Y_2007) FROM NUM_ACCIDENT_DEATHS_KOSHA_I_MIDDLE_CLASSIFICATION)
SELECT T1.SORTATION, T1.Y_2021 FROM NUM_WORKERS_KOSHA_I_MIDDLE_CLASSIFICATION AS T1 JOIN NUM_ACCIDENT_DEATHS_KOSHA_I_MIDDLE_CLASSIFICATION AS T2 ON T1.SORTATION = T2.SORTATION WHERE T2.Y_2021 > (SELECT MAX(Y_2021) FROM NUM_ACCIDENT_DEATHS_KOSHA_I_MIDDLE_CLASSIFICATION) AND T2.Y_2004 > T2.Y_2021 AND T1.Y_2020 >= 327413
SELECT SORTATION FROM NUM_ACCIDENT_DEATHS_KOSHA_I_MIDDLE_CLASSIFICATION WHERE Y_2011 >= 100 AND SORTATION IN (SELECT SORTATION FROM NUM_WORKERS_KOSHA_I_MIDDLE_CLASSIFICATION WHERE Y_2011 >= 1000000)
SELECT T1.Y_2010, T1.SORTATION FROM NUM_ACCIDENT_DEATHS_KOSHA_I_MIDDLE_CLASSIFICATION AS T1 JOIN (SELECT AVG(Y_2004) AS AVG_WORKERS FROM NUM_WORKERS_KOSHA_I_MIDDLE_CLASSIFICATION) AS T2 ON T1.Y_2004 > T2.AVG_WORKERS
SELECT T1.SORTATION, T1.LARGE_INDUSTRY FROM NUM_WORKERS_KOSHA_I_MIDDLE_CLASSIFICATION AS T1 JOIN NUM_ACCIDENT_DEATHS_KOSHA_I_MIDDLE_CLASSIFICATION AS T2 ON T1.SORTATION = T2.SORTATION WHERE T2.Y_2021 >= 10 OR T1.Y_2011 <= 10000
SELECT SORTATION, LARGE_INDUSTRY FROM NUM_WORKERS_KOSHA_I_MIDDLE_CLASSIFICATION WHERE Y_2006 < Y_2007 AND Y_2010 > Y_2012;
SELECT SORTATION, LARGE_INDUSTRY FROM NUM_WORKERS_KOSHA_I_MIDDLE_CLASSIFICATION WHERE Y_2016 >= 16 OR Y_2016 <= 5000
SELECT LARGE_INDUSTRY, SORTATION FROM NUM_WORKERS_KOSHA_I_MIDDLE_CLASSIFICATION WHERE Y_2018 > (SELECT AVG(Y_2018) FROM NUM_WORKERS_KOSHA_I_MIDDLE_CLASSIFICATION) AND SORTATION IN (SELECT SORTATION FROM NUM_ACCIDENT_DEATHS_KOSHA_I_MIDDLE_CLASSIFICATION WHERE Y_2018 > (SELECT AVG(Y_2018) FROM NUM_ACCIDENT_DEATHS_KOSHA_I_MIDDLE_CLASSIFICATION))
SELECT Y_2010 FROM NUM_WORKERS_KOSHA_I_MIDDLE_CLASSIFICATION WHERE SORTATION LIKE '%제조%'
SELECT T1.SORTATION, T1.Y_2020 FROM NUM_WORKERS_KOSHA_I_MIDDLE_CLASSIFICATION AS T1 JOIN NUM_ACCIDENT_DEATHS_KOSHA_I_MIDDLE_CLASSIFICATION AS T2 ON T1.SORTATION = T2.SORTATION WHERE T2.Y_2018 >= 14 OR T1.Y_2017 < (SELECT AVG(Y_2017) FROM NUM_WORKERS_KOSHA_I_MIDDLE_CLASSIFICATION) AND T1.Y_2017 < T1.Y_2016

SELECT AVG(H_02E) AS AVG_2H_SUPPLY, AVG(H_03F) AS AVG_3H_SUPPLY FROM KPX_TRANSMISSION_PW_STATION_HOURLY_INFO WHERE H_01D <= 50000 OR H_01D >= 60000

SELECT YEAR FROM NUM_SU_CO_EMPLOYEE_SIZE_KOSMES_DEV_TECH_COMMERCIALIZATION_FUND AS T1 JOIN NUM_SU_CO_KOSMES_DEV_TECH_COMMERCIALIZATION_FUND_COLLATERAL AS T2 ON T1.YEAR = T2.YEAR WHERE T1.LESS_THAN_50 > (SELECT AVG(LESS_THAN_20) FROM NUM_SU_CO_EMPLOYEE_SIZE_KOSMES_DEV_TECH_COMMERCIALIZATION_FUND) OR T2.REAL_ESTATE <= 4 ORDER BY T1.YEAR ASC
SELECT T1.YEAR FROM NUM_SU_CO_EMPLOYEE_SIZE_KOSMES_DEV_TECH_COMMERCIALIZATION_FUND AS T1 JOIN NUM_SU_CO_KOSMES_DEV_TECH_COMMERCIALIZATION_FUND_COLLATERAL AS T2 ON T1.YEAR = T2.YEAR WHERE T1.LESS_THAN_300 >= 8 OR T2.CREDIT >= 800
SELECT T1.YEAR FROM NUM_SU_CO_KOSMES_DEV_TECH_COMMERCIALIZATION_FUND_COLLATERAL AS T1 JOIN NUM_SU_CO_EMPLOYEE_SIZE_KOSMES_DEV_TECH_COMMERCIALIZATION_FUND AS T2 ON T1.YEAR = T2.YEAR WHERE T2.LESS_THAN_50 > T2.LESS_THAN_20 AND T1.REAL_ESTATE >= 5
SELECT YEAR FROM NUM_SU_CO_KOSMES_DEV_TECH_COMMERCIALIZATION_FUND_COLLATERAL WHERE INTELLECTUAL_PROPERTY = 3 OR (SELECT LESS_THAN_300 FROM NUM_SU_CO_EMPLOYEE_SIZE_KOSMES_DEV_TECH_COMMERCIALIZATION_FUND WHERE YEAR = NUM_SU_CO_KOSMES_DEV_TECH_COMMERCIALIZATION_FUND_COLLATERAL.YEAR) <= 7
SELECT T1.YEAR FROM NUM_SU_CO_KOSMES_DEV_TECH_COMMERCIALIZATION_FUND_COLLATERAL AS T1 JOIN NUM_SU_CO_EMPLOYEE_SIZE_KOSMES_DEV_TECH_COMMERCIALIZATION_FUND AS T2 ON T1.YEAR = T2.YEAR WHERE T2.LESS_THAN_300 = 8 OR T1.TELLECTUAL_PROPERTY >= 6
SELECT T1.YEAR FROM NUM_SU_CO_KOSMES_DEV_TECH_COMMERCIALIZATION_FUND_COLLATERAL AS T1 JOIN NUM_SU_CO_EMPLOYEE_SIZE_KOSMES_DEV_TECH_COMMERCIALIZATION_FUND AS T2 ON T1.YEAR = T2.YEAR WHERE T1.LETTER_GUARANTEE > (SELECT AVG(LETTER_GUARANTEE) FROM NUM_SU_CO_KOSMES_DEV_TECH_COMMERCIALIZATION_FUND_COLLATERAL) AND T1.TELLECTUAL_PROPERTY > (SELECT AVG(TELLECTUAL_PROPERTY) FROM NUM_SU_CO_KOSMES_DEV_TECH_COMMERCIALIZATION_FUND_COLLATERAL) AND T2.LESS_THAN_5 < 30;
SELECT "YEAR" FROM NUM_SU_CO_EMPLOYEE_SIZE_KOSMES_DEV_TECH_COMMERCIALIZATION_FUND WHERE OVER_300 = 8
SELECT T2.YEAR FROM NUM_SU_CO_KOSMES_DEV_TECH_COMMERCIALIZATION_FUND_COLLATERAL AS T1 JOIN NUM_SU_CO_EMPLOYEE_SIZE_KOSMES_DEV_TECH_COMMERCIALIZATION_FUND AS T2 ON T1.YEAR = T2.YEAR WHERE T1.LETTER_GUARANTEE = 3 OR T2.LESS_THAN_20 >= 100 ORDER BY T2.LESS_THAN_5
SELECT YEAR FROM NUM_SU_CO_EMPLOYEE_SIZE_KOSMES_DEV_TECH_COMMERCIALIZATION_FUND WHERE LESS_THAN_10 < (SELECT AVG(LESS_THAN_10) FROM NUM_SU_CO_EMPLOYEE_SIZE_KOSMES_DEV_TECH_COMMERCIALIZATION_FUND) OR LESS_THAN_20 < (SELECT AVG(LESS_THAN_20) FROM NUM_SU_CO_EMPLOYEE_SIZE_KOSMES_DEV_TECH_COMMERCIALIZATION_FUND) GROUP BY YEAR
SELECT YEAR FROM NUM_SU_CO_EMPLOYEE_SIZE_KOSMES_DEV_TECH_COMMERCIALIZATION_FUND WHERE LESS_THAN_20 = 100 OR LESS_THAN_20 < 20
SELECT YEAR FROM NUM_SU_CO_EMPLOYEE_SIZE_KOSMES_DEV_TECH_COMMERCIALIZATION_FUND WHERE LESS_THAN_10 > 0 GROUP BY YEAR ORDER BY COUNT(CREDIT) DESC LIMIT 1

SELECT DISTINCT YEAR FROM NUM_SU_CO_KOSMES_DEV_TECH_COMMERCIALIZATION_FUND_COLLATERAL WHERE INTELLECTUAL_PROPERTY = 1 AND OTHERS = 1

SELECT ORNAMENT, QUANTITY FROM SELMETRO_HISTORICAL_CULTURE_ARTS_DECORATION_STS WHERE LINE = 5 AND LOCATION = '대합실'
SELECT T1.LINE, T1.STATION_NAME, T2.ORNAMENT FROM SELMETRO_ELEVATOR_I_INFO AS T1 JOIN SELMETRO_HISTORICAL_CULTURE_ARTS_DECORATION_STS AS T2 ON T1.LINE = T2.LINE AND T1.STATION_NAME = T2.STATION_NAME WHERE T1.INSTALLATION_LOCATION = '대합실' AND T2.QUANTITY >= 2 AND T1.AORY = '서울'
SELECT ORNAMENT, INSTALLATION_LOCATION FROM SELMETRO_HISTORICAL_CULTURE_ARTS_DECORATION_STS WHERE STATION_NAME LIKE '%을지%'
SELECT ELEVATOR_NUMBER FROM SELMETRO_ELEVATOR_I_INFO WHERE STATION_NAME IN (SELECT STATION_NAME FROM SELMETRO_HISTORICAL_CULTURE_ARTS_DECORATION_STS WHERE QUANTITY >= 5 AND LOCATION = '출구')
SELECT OPERATING_SECTION FROM SELMETRO_ELEVATOR_I_INFO WHERE STATION_NAME IN (SELECT STATION_NAME FROM SELMETRO_HISTORICAL_CULTURE_ARTS_DECORATION_STS WHERE WRITER = '김씨' AND QUANTITY < (SELECT AVG(QUANTITY) FROM SELMETRO_HISTORICAL_CULTURE_ARTS_DECORATION_STS))
SELECT STATION_NAME, ORNAMENT FROM SELMETRO_HISTORICAL_CULTURE_ARTS_DECORATION_STS WHERE TYPE = '장식벽' AND QUANTITY > (SELECT AVG(QUANTITY) FROM SELMETRO_HISTORICAL_CULTURE_ARTS_DECORATION_STS)
SELECT LINE, STATION_NAME, ORNAMENT FROM SELMETRO_ELEVATOR_I_INFO JOIN SELMETRO_HISTORICAL_CULTURE_ARTS_DECORATION_STS ON SELMETRO_ELEVATOR_I_INFO.LINE = SELMETRO_HISTORICAL_CULTURE_ARTS_DECORATION_STS.LINE AND SELMETRO_ELEVATOR_I_INFO.STATION_NAME = SELMETRO_HISTORICAL_CULTURE_ARTS_DECORATION_STS.STATION_NAME WHERE INSTALLATION_LOCATION = '승강장' AND QUANTITY >= 4
SELECT T1.LINE, T1.STATION_NAME, T2.ORNAMENT FROM SELMETRO_ELEVATOR_I_INFO AS T1 JOIN SELMETRO_HISTORICAL_CULTURE_ARTS_DECORATION_STS AS T2 ON T1.LINE = T2.LINE AND T1.STATION_NAME = T2.STATION_NAME WHERE T1.INSTALLATION_LOCATION = '통로층' AND T2.TYPE = '조형물'
SELECT T1.STATION_NAME, T1.INSTALLATION_LOCATION FROM SELMETRO_HISTORICAL_CULTURE_ARTS_DECORATION_STS AS T1 JOIN SELMETRO_ELEVATOR_I_INFO AS T2 ON T1.LINE = T2.LINE AND T1.STATION_NAME = T2.STATION_NAME WHERE T1.ORNAMENT = '조형물' OR T1.QUANTITY >= 6
SELECT T1.STATION_NAME, T2.LOCATION FROM SELMETRO_ELEVATOR_I_INFO AS T1 JOIN SELMETRO_HISTORICAL_CULTURE_ARTS_DECORATION_STS AS T2 ON T1.LINE = T2.LINE AND T1.STATION_NAME = T2.STATION_NAME WHERE T1.ELEVATOR_NUMBER = '3' OR T1.OPERATING_SECTION LIKE 'F1%'
SELECT STATION_NAME FROM SELMETRO_ELEVATOR_I_INFO WHERE LINE = '5'
SELECT STATION_NAME FROM SELMETRO_ELEVATOR_I_INFO WHERE STATION_NAME LIKE '%3%' OR STATION_NAME LIKE '%공항%' GROUP BY STATION_NAME
SELECT STATION_NAME FROM SELMETRO_ELEVATOR_I_INFO WHERE INSTALLATION_LOCATION = '승강장' AND ELEVATOR_NUMBER LIKE '%4'
SELECT STATION_NAME, LOCATION FROM SELMETRO_HISTORICAL_CULTURE_ARTS_DECORATION_STS GROUP BY STATION_NAME, LOCATION HAVING COUNT(ORNAMENT) >= 1
SELECT STATION_NAME FROM SELMETRO_HISTORICAL_CULTURE_ARTS_DECORATION_STS WHERE ORNAMENT LIKE '파%' OR ELEVATOR_NUMBER LIKE '%33%' ORDER BY STATION_NAME ASC
SELECT INSTALLATION_LOCATION FROM SELMETRO_ELEVATOR_I_INFO WHERE STATION_NAME LIKE '%대로' OR LINE = '5'
SELECT INSTALLATION_LOCATION FROM SELMETRO_ELEVATOR_I_INFO WHERE STATION_NAME IN (SELECT STATION_NAME FROM SELMETRO_HISTORICAL_CULTURE_ARTS_DECORATION_STS WHERE TYPE = '담장선' AND ORNAMENT = '장식벽' AND LOCATION = '한국')
SELECT DISTINCT STATION_NAME FROM SELMETRO_ELEVATOR_I_INFO WHERE INSTALLATION_LOCATION LIKE '%시점%' OR EQUIPMENT = '육의전'
SELECT DISTINCT T1.STATION_NAME FROM SELMETRO_HISTORICAL_CULTURE_ARTS_DECORATION_STS AS T1 JOIN SELMETRO_ELEVATOR_I_INFO AS T2 ON T1.STATION_NAME = T2.STATION_NAME WHERE T1.QUANTITY = 1 OR T2.INSTALLATION_LOCATION = '외부'
SELECT DISTINCT STATION_NAME FROM SELMETRO_HISTORICAL_CULTURE_ARTS_DECORATION_STS WHERE QUANTITY = 1 OR LINE = 3
SELECT STATION_NAME FROM SELMETRO_HISTORICAL_CULTURE_ARTS_DECORATION_STS WHERE ORNAMENT LIKE '%전' AND TYPE = '조형물'
SELECT STATION_NAME FROM SELMETRO_ELEVATOR_I_INFO WHERE ELEVATOR_NUMBER LIKE '%6' AND STATION_NAME IN ( SELECT STATION_NAME FROM SELMETRO_HISTORICAL_CULTURE_ARTS_DECORATION_STS WHERE ORNAMENT LIKE '%한국%' )
SELECT DISTINCT STATION_NAME FROM SELMETRO_HISTORICAL_CULTURE_ARTS_DECORATION_STS WHERE ORNAMENT LIKE '%한국%'

SELECT BPLCNM FROM L_O_C_A_L_D_A_T_A_030506_G_B WHERE APVPERMYMD = '198903' AND TRDSTATENM = '강북구 일반 게임 제공업'
SELECT BPLCNM FROM L_O_C_A_L_D_A_T_A_030506_G_B WHERE SITEWHLADDR LIKE '%미아동%'
SELECT BPLCNM, SITEWHLADDR FROM L_O_C_A_L_D_A_T_A_030506_G_B WHERE APVPERMYMD LIKE '2022%' AND DTLSTATENM = '영업중' ORDER BY BPLCNM;
SELECT Y FROM L_O_C_A_L_D_A_T_A_030506_G_B WHERE NEARENVNM != '주변유흥업소밀집지역'
SELECT SITETEL FROM L_O_C_A_L_D_A_T_A_030506_G_B WHERE BPLCNM = '신세대오락실'
SELECT DCBYMD FROM L_O_C_A_L_D_A_T_A_030506_G_B WHERE BPLCNM = '삼원'
SELECT SITETEL FROM L_O_C_A_L_D_A_T_A_030506_G_B WHERE BPLCNM = '대성'
SELECT SITETEL FROM L_O_C_A_L_D_A_T_A_030506_G_B WHERE SITEPOSTNO = '142877'
SELECT FACILAR FROM L_O_C_A_L_D_A_T_A_030506_G_B WHERE SITEWHLADDR LIKE '%우이동%'
SELECT APVPERMYMD FROM L_O_C_A_L_D_A_T_A_030506_G_B WHERE NEARENVNM = '유흥업소밀집지역' ORDER BY APVPERMYMD DESC;
SELECT BPLCNM, X FROM L_O_C_A_L_D_A_T_A_030506_G_B WHERE NEARENVNM = '유흥업소밀집'
SELECT BPLCNM FROM L_O_C_A_L_D_A_T_A_030506_G_B WHERE DTLSTATENM != '등록취소' ORDER BY BPLCNM
SELECT BPLCNM FROM L_O_C_A_L_D_A_T_A_030506_G_B WHERE DTLSTATENM = '직권말소'
